**OpenAI Codex**

<permissions instructions>
Filesystem sandboxing defines which files can be read or written. `sandbox_mode` is `workspace-write`: The sandbox permits reading files, and editing files in `cwd` and `writable_roots`. Editing files in other directories requires approval. Network access is restricted.
# Escalation Requests

Commands are run outside the sandbox if they are approved by the user, or match an existing rule that allows it to run unrestricted. The command string is split into independent command segments at shell control operators, including but not limited to:

- Pipes: |
- Logical operators: &&, ||
- Command separators: ;
- Subshell boundaries: (...), $(...)

Each resulting segment is evaluated independently for sandbox restrictions and approval requirements.

Example:

git pull | tee output.txt

This is treated as two command segments:

["git", "pull"]

["tee", "output.txt"]

Commands that use more advanced shell features like redirection (>, >>, <), substitutions ($(...), ...), environment variables (FOO=bar), or wildcard patterns (*, ?) will not be evaluated against rules, to limit the scope of what an approved rule allows.

## How to request escalation

IMPORTANT: To request approval to execute a command that will require escalated privileges:

- Provide the `sandbox_permissions` parameter with the value `"require_escalated"`
- Include a short question asking the user if they want to allow the action in `justification` parameter. e.g. "Do you want to download and install dependencies for this project?"
- Optionally suggest a `prefix_rule` - this will be shown to the user with an option to persist the rule approval for future sessions.

If you run a command that is important to solving the user's query, but it fails because of sandboxing or with a likely sandbox-related network error (for example DNS/host resolution, registry/index access, or dependency download failure), rerun the command with "require_escalated". ALWAYS proceed to use the `justification` parameter - do not message the user before requesting approval for the command.

## When to request escalation

While commands are running inside the sandbox, here are some scenarios that will require escalation outside the sandbox:

- You need to run a command that writes to a directory that requires it (e.g. running tests that write to /var)
- You need to run a GUI app (e.g., open/xdg-open/osascript) to open browsers or files.
- If you run a command that is important to solving the user's query, but it fails because of sandboxing or with a likely sandbox-related network error (for example DNS/host resolution, registry/index access, or dependency download failure), rerun the command with `require_escalated`. ALWAYS proceed to use the `sandbox_permissions` and `justification` parameters. do not message the user before requesting approval for the command.
- You are about to take a potentially destructive action such as an `rm` or `git reset` that the user did not explicitly ask for.
- Be judicious with escalating, but if completing the user's request requires it, you should do so - don't try and circumvent approvals by using other tools.

## prefix_rule guidance

When choosing a `prefix_rule`, request one that will allow you to fulfill similar requests from the user in the future without re-requesting escalation. It should be categorical and reasonably scoped to similar capabilities. You should rarely pass the entire command into `prefix_rule`.

### Banned prefix_rules 
Avoid requesting overly broad prefixes that the user would be ill-advised to approve. For example, do not request ["python3"], ["python", "-"], or other similar prefixes that would allow arbitrary scripting.
NEVER provide a prefix_rule argument for destructive commands like rm.
NEVER provide a prefix_rule if your command uses a heredoc or herestring. 

### Examples
Good examples of prefixes:
- ["npm", "run", "dev"]
- ["gh", "pr", "check"]
- ["cargo", "test"]


## Approved command prefixes
The following prefix rules have already been approved: - ["E:\\NEW\\MY_HARMONY\\hvigorw.bat"]
- ["git", "-C", "E:/new/my_harmony"]
- ["C:\\Program Files\\PowerShell\\7\\pwsh.exe", "-Command", "Remove-Item -Recurse -Force C:\\Users\\AI008\\.hvigor\\project_caches\\821173b1a6052304d2facf3673d35df3\\workspace; D:\\harmSdk\\command-line-tools\\bin\\hvigorw.bat assembleApp"]
- ["Remove-Item", "-LiteralPath", "entry/src/main/ets/pages/level/LevelDataTable.ets.codex_delete", "-Force"]
 The writable root is `E:\goTest`.

If you absolutely must ask a question because the answer cannot be discovered from local context and a reasonable assumption would be risky, ask the user directly with a concise plain-text question. ### How to use skills
- Discovery: The list above is the skills available in this session (name + description + file path). Skill bodies live on disk at the listed paths.
- Trigger rules: If the user names a skill (with `$SkillName` or plain text) OR the task clearly matches a skill's description shown above, you must use that skill for that turn. Multiple mentions mean use them all. Do not carry skills across turns unless re-mentioned.
- Missing/blocked: If a named skill isn't in the list or the path can't be read, say so briefly and continue with the best fallback.
- How to use a skill (progressive disclosure):
  1) After deciding to use a skill, open its `SKILL.md`. Read only enough to follow the workflow.
  2) When `SKILL.md` references relative paths (e.g., `scripts/foo.py`), resolve them relative to the skill directory listed above first, and only consider other paths if needed.
  3) If `SKILL.md` points to extra folders such as `references/`, load only the specific files needed for the request; don't bulk-load everything.
  4) If `scripts/` exist, prefer running or patching them instead of retyping large code blocks.
  5) If `assets/` or templates exist, reuse them instead of recreating from scratch.
- Coordination and sequencing:
  - If multiple skills apply, choose the minimal set that covers the request and state the order you'll use them.

A plugin is a local bundle of skills, MCP servers, and apps. Below is the list of plugins that are enabled and available in this session.
### Available plugins
- `Browser`: Browser / browser-use plugin Aliases: @browser, @browser-use, browser-use, Browser, in-app browser. Use Browser, the Codex in-app browser, when the user asks to open, inspect, navigate, test, click, type, or screenshot local web targets such as localhost, 127.0.0.1, ::1, file:// URLs, or the current in-app browser tab. After significant frontend changes to a local app, use Browser to open the relevant local target when it is known or obvious, unless the user asks for another browser tool. For requests like "open localhost:3000" or "open to localhost:4000", navigate the in-app browser to http://localhost:3000 or http://localhost:4000. Do not satisfy explicit @browser or @browser-use requests with macOS `open`, shell commands, or generic web browsing unless the user asks for another browser tool or approves a fallback.

- Skill naming: If a plugin contributes skills, those skill entries are prefixed with `plugin_name:` in the Skills list.

1. `go/ohos/Tcp/ctcpclient.go`

     - `cTCPHCWAMSimulatedPulseOff = 0x0114`

     - `cTCPHCWAMGetWAMInfo = 0x0F00`
   - Important decision: frontend `wamGetInfo` should map to **0x0110 `HC_WAM_CMD_WEIGHT_ON`**, matching 48 startup behavior, not `0x0F00` version info.

     - `SendWAMGlobalWeightInfoData`
     - `sendWAMCommand`
   - Added ID normalization:
     - `normalizeWAMDestID`: converts FSM/base ids to WAM base like `0x01D0`
     - `normalizeWAMChannelDestID`: converts base + `channelIndex` to channel id like `0x01D1/0x01D2`; if `DestID` already has low nibble nonzero, leaves it as channel id.
   - Added encoders:
     - `encodeWeightBaseInfoPayload`

     - map `source.Weights[]` to `target.weights[]`
     - likely add interfaces/types or use existing `StGlobalJson` where `GWeight?: object`, `Weights?: object[]`.
   - Then update `GlobalDataInterface.updateGlobalConfig()` to push a `StWeightGlobal` cache from `config.gweight/config.weights`, so `WeightSettingsPage.getWeightGlobalSnapshot()` has data even before WAM direct `weightGlobal` topic:
     - create `StWeightGlobal`
     - `nWAMId = (deviceId & 0x0F00) | (ConstPreDefine.WAM_ID & 0x00FF)` or equivalent
     - copy `config.gweight` and `config.weights`
     - call `updateWeightGlobal(wamId, weightGlobal)` or set map then notify.
   - This addresses user’s exact complaint “全是空的” when only FSM `StGlobal` has arrived.

2. **Possibly add direct fallback in `HarmonyWebSocketClient.handleStGlobalData` instead of `GlobalDataInterface`**
   - Alternative: after mapping StGlobal, build `StWeightGlobal` directly from raw `StGlobalJson.GWeight/Weights` and call `updateWeightGlobal`.
   - Prefer `StGlobalJsonMapper + GlobalDataInterface` because it centralizes StGlobal-derived config and matches 48.

3. Verify with light checks only:
   - `git -C E:/goTest diff --check`
   - `git -C E:/new/my_harmony diff --check`
   - `rg` for new symbols.
   - Do **not** run builds/tests unless user explicitly asks.

Caution:
- `git -C E:/goTest diff --stat` includes lots of pre-existing dirty changes (waylog, EntryAbility, Index, existing Go changes). Do not revert them.
- Go files may show LF->CRLF warnings; ignore unless user asks.

**OpenAI Codex**

<permissions instructions>
Filesystem sandboxing defines which files can be read or written. `sandbox_mode` is `workspace-write`: The sandbox permits reading files, and editing files in `cwd` and `writable_roots`. Editing files in other directories requires approval. Network access is restricted.
# Escalation Requests

Commands are run outside the sandbox if they are approved by the user, or match an existing rule that allows it to run unrestricted. The command string is split into independent command segments at shell control operators, including but not limited to:

- Pipes: |
- Logical operators: &&, ||
- Command separators: ;
- Subshell boundaries: (...), $(...)

Each resulting segment is evaluated independently for sandbox restrictions and approval requirements.

Example:

git pull | tee output.txt

This is treated as two command segments:

["git", "pull"]

["tee", "output.txt"]

Commands that use more advanced shell features like redirection (>, >>, <), substitutions ($(...), ...), environment variables (FOO=bar), or wildcard patterns (*, ?) will not be evaluated against rules, to limit the scope of what an approved rule allows.

## How to request escalation

IMPORTANT: To request approval to execute a command that will require escalated privileges:

- Provide the `sandbox_permissions` parameter with the value `"require_escalated"`
- Include a short question asking the user if they want to allow the action in `justification` parameter. e.g. "Do you want to download and install dependencies for this project?"
- Optionally suggest a `prefix_rule` - this will be shown to the user with an option to persist the rule approval for future sessions.

If you run a command that is important to solving the user's query, but it fails because of sandboxing or with a likely sandbox-related network error (for example DNS/host resolution, registry/index access, or dependency download failure), rerun the command with "require_escalated". ALWAYS proceed to use the `justification` parameter - do not message the user before requesting approval for the command.

## When to request escalation

While commands are running inside the sandbox, here are some scenarios that will require escalation outside the sandbox:

- You need to run a command that writes to a directory that requires it (e.g. running tests that write to /var)
- You need to run a GUI app (e.g., open/xdg-open/osascript) to open browsers or files.
- If you run a command that is important to solving the user's query, but it fails because of sandboxing or with a likely sandbox-related network error (for example DNS/host resolution, registry/index access, or dependency download failure), rerun the command with `require_escalated`. ALWAYS proceed to use the `sandbox_permissions` and `justification` parameters. do not message the user before requesting approval for the command.
- You are about to take a potentially destructive action such as an `rm` or `git reset` that the user did not explicitly ask for.
- Be judicious with escalating, but if completing the user's request requires it, you should do so - don't try and circumvent approvals by using other tools.

## prefix_rule guidance

When choosing a `prefix_rule`, request one that will allow you to fulfill similar requests from the user in the future without re-requesting escalation. It should be categorical and reasonably scoped to similar capabilities. You should rarely pass the entire command into `prefix_rule`.

### Banned prefix_rules 
Avoid requesting overly broad prefixes that the user would be ill-advised to approve. For example, do not request ["python3"], ["python", "-"], or other similar prefixes that would allow arbitrary scripting.
NEVER provide a prefix_rule argument for destructive commands like rm.
NEVER provide a prefix_rule if your command uses a heredoc or herestring. 

### Examples
Good examples of prefixes:
- ["npm", "run", "dev"]
- ["gh", "pr", "check"]
- ["cargo", "test"]


## Approved command prefixes
The following prefix rules have already been approved: - ["E:\\NEW\\MY_HARMONY\\hvigorw.bat"]
- ["git", "-C", "E:/new/my_harmony"]
- ["C:\\Program Files\\PowerShell\\7\\pwsh.exe", "-Command", "Remove-Item -Recurse -Force C:\\Users\\AI008\\.hvigor\\project_caches\\821173b1a6052304d2facf3673d35df3\\workspace; D:\\harmSdk\\command-line-tools\\bin\\hvigorw.bat assembleApp"]
- ["Remove-Item", "-LiteralPath", "entry/src/main/ets/pages/level/LevelDataTable.ets.codex_delete", "-Force"]
 The writable root is `E:\goTest`.

### How to use skills
- Discovery: The list above is the skills available in this session (name + description + file path). Skill bodies live on disk at the listed paths.
- Trigger rules: If the user names a skill (with `$SkillName` or plain text) OR the task clearly matches a skill's description shown above, you must use that skill for that turn. Multiple mentions mean use them all. Do not carry skills across turns unless re-mentioned.
- Missing/blocked: If a named skill isn't in the list or the path can't be read, say so briefly and continue with the best fallback.
- How to use a skill (progressive disclosure):
  1) After deciding to use a skill, open its `SKILL.md`. Read only enough to follow the workflow.
  2) When `SKILL.md` references relative paths (e.g., `scripts/foo.py`), resolve them relative to the skill directory listed above first, and only consider other paths if needed.
  3) If `SKILL.md` points to extra folders such as `references/`, load only the specific files needed for the request; don't bulk-load everything.
  4) If `scripts/` exist, prefer running or patching them instead of retyping large code blocks.
  5) If `assets/` or templates exist, reuse them instead of recreating from scratch.
- Coordination and sequencing:
  - If multiple skills apply, choose the minimal set that covers the request and state the order you'll use them.
  - Announce which skill(s) you're using and why (one short line). If you skip an obvious skill, say why.
- Context hygiene:
  - Keep context small: summarize long sections instead of pasting them; only load extra files when needed.
  - Avoid deep reference-chasing: prefer opening only files directly linked from `SKILL.md` unless you're blocked.
  - When variants exist (frameworks, providers, domains), pick only the relevant reference file(s) and note that choice.
- Safety and fallback: If a skill can't be applied cleanly (missing files, unclear instructions), state the issue, pick the next-best approach, and continue.
</skills_instructions><plugins_instructions>
## Plugins
A plugin is a local bundle of skills, MCP servers, and apps. Below is the list of plugins that are enabled and available in this session.
### Available plugins
- `Browser`: Browser / browser-use plugin Aliases: @browser, @browser-use, browser-use, Browser, in-app browser. Use Browser, the Codex in-app browser, when the user asks to open, inspect, navigate, test, click, type, or screenshot local web targets such as localhost, 127.0.0.1, ::1, file:// URLs, or the current in-app browser tab. After significant frontend changes to a local app, use Browser to open the relevant local target when it is known or obvious, unless the user asks for another browser tool. For requests like "open localhost:3000" or "open to localhost:4000", navigate the in-app browser to http://localhost:3000 or http://localhost:4000. Do not satisfy explicit @browser or @browser-use requests with macOS `open`, shell commands, or generic web browsing unless the user asks for another browser tool or approves a fallback.
### How to use plugins
- Discovery: The list above is the plugins available in this session.
- Skill naming: If a plugin contributes skills, those skill entries are prefixed with `plugin_name:` in the Skills list.
- Trigger rules: If the user explicitly names a plugin, prefer capabilities associated with that plugin for that turn.
- Relationship to capabilities: Plugins are not invoked directly. Use their underlying skills, MCP tools, and app tools to help solve the task.
- Preference: When a relevant plugin is available, prefer using capabilities associated with that plugin over standalone capabilities that provide similar functionality.
- Missing/blocked: If the user requests a plugin that is not listed above, or the plugin does not have relevant callable capabilities for the task, say so briefly and continue with the best fallback.
</plugins_instructions>

- [Structures.ets](E:/new/my_harmony/entry/src/main/ets/protocol/Structures.ets:858) 给 `StGlobal` 补了 `gweight` 和 `weights`

- [GlobalDataInterface.ets](E:/new/my_harmony/entry/src/main/ets/protocol/GlobalDataInterface.ets:1582) 收到 `StGlobal` 后，会同步成 `weightGlobal` 缓存给重量设置页面用

**OpenAI Codex**

没事没事，我在，刚刚只是去确认链路了。

如果你说的是**重量设置页面**的“立即生效”，是的，它就是数据下发，不是单纯改 UI。

现在点击后走这里：

[WeightSettingsPage.ets](E:/new/my_harmony/entry/src/main/ets/components/dialogs/pages/WeightSettingsPage.ets:617)

它会下发两份数据：

1. `sendWamWeightInfoTracked`
   通道参数，下发 `StWeightBaseInfo`，命令是 `0x011D`

2. `sendWamGlobalWeightInfoTracked`
   全局重量参数，下发 `StGlobalWeightBaseInfo`，命令是 `0x011C`

然后 ArkTS 通过 WebSocket 发给 Go：

[HarmonyWebSocketClient.ets](E:/new/my_harmony/entry/src/main/ets/utils/network/HarmonyWebSocketClient.ets:782)

Go 后端再转成 WAM 指令发给 WAM 下位机。

所以结论是：**是下发**。  
但是如果现在没有连 WAM 板子，可能表现为：前端发出去了、Go 收到了，但真正到 WAM 那一步失败或者没有回读，所以页面可能又显示旧值。

**OpenAI Codex**

现在**代码层面已经会下发**，但我不能直接确认你这一次现场是否真的成功，因为我没看到当前运行日志。

要分两层看：

- **发到 Go 后端成功**：ArkTS `sendText()` 成功，页面会显示 `参数已发送`
- **WAM 下位机真正接收成功**：还要看 Go 返回的 ack/result

你看日志里有没有这两类：

```text
sending saveWamWeightInfo ... cmd=0x011D
sending saveWamGlobalWeightInfo ... cmd=0x011C
```

然后重点看 ack：

```text
command ack ... ok=true result=0 cmd=0x011D
command ack ... ok=true result=0 cmd=0x011C
```

如果 `result=0`，才算真正下发成功。  
如果是 `result=-1`，通常就是 WAM 没连上、IP/端口不通，或者下位机没响应。

所以现在结论是：**前端已经发了；是否真正生效，要看 `0x011C / 0x011D` 的 ack result。**

**OpenAI Codex**

现在点“立即生效”后，后端应该会出现类似：

```text
WebSocket 收到 saveWamWeightInfo: dest=0x01D1, channelIndex=0, StWeightBaseInfo{FGADParam=[...], FTemperatureParams=..., WaveInterval=[...]}
WebSocket saveWamWeightInfo: sending WAM cmd=0x011D, dest=0x01D1, target=...:1299, payload=16 bytes
WebSocket saveWamWeightInfo success/failed: ...
```

以及全局参数：

```text
WebSocket 收到 saveWamGlobalWeightInfo: dest=0x01D0, StGlobalWeightBaseInfo{FFilterParam=..., AD_Filter_ALG=..., ...}
WebSocket saveWamGlobalWeightInfo: sending WAM cmd=0x011C, dest=0x01D0, target=...:1299, payload=... bytes
WebSocket saveWamGlobalWeightInfo success/failed: ...
```

这样就能分清楚三件事：

1. 前端有没有发到 Go：看 `WebSocket 收到 ...`
2. Go 有没有转发到 WAM：看 `sending WAM cmd=0x011C/0x011D`
3. WAM 是否成功：看 `success` 或 `failed result=-1`

**OpenAI Codex**

从日志看：通道参数 `0x011D` 已经发成功了，全局重量参数 `0x011C` 失败了；同时 `wamGetInfo 0x0110` 成功并收到了 `WAM__CMD_WEIGHT_INFO(0x0120)` 回包。你问的“内信号源/测试果杯”我去对一下 48 的命令定义和调用位置，避免靠名字猜。

---


**OpenAI Codex**

48 这里也没建 codegraph，我直接用全文搜索。

---


**OpenAI Codex**

搜到了：48 的重量设置页里，内信号源是发给 WAM 的 `HC_WAM_CMD_SIMULATEDPULSE_ON/OFF`，测试果杯在 48 里是发给 FSM 的 `HC_CMD_TEST_CUP_ON/OFF`。我看一下附近逻辑。

---


**OpenAI Codex**

顺便发现一个关键差异：48 的“测试果杯”在重量设置页不是发 WAM `0x0115/0x0116`，而是发 FSM 的 `HC_CMD_TEST_CUP_ON/OFF`，并且只在测试模式下发。你现在问用途，我先给你讲清楚这个差异。

---


**OpenAI Codex**

48 里还有一个行为：离开重量设置页时会自动关闭内信号源和测试果杯，防止测试状态一直挂着。这个我们后面最好也按 48 补。

---


**OpenAI Codex**

从日志看，你这次链路是这样的：

- `0x011D` 通道重量参数：成功发到 WAM
- `0x011C` 全局重量参数：失败，`result=-1`
- `0x0110` 获取 WAM 参数：成功，而且 WAM 回了 `0x0120`

**内信号源**
这是 WAM 的“模拟脉冲/内部触发源”。

48 里对应：

```text
HC_WAM_CMD_SIMULATEDPULSE_ON  = 0x0113
HC_WAM_CMD_SIMULATEDPULSE_OFF = 0x0114
```

用途：不用真实外部果杯信号，让 WAM 自己产生内部触发，用来调试称重、标定、看波形/数据追踪。48 里打开内信号源时，还会把数据追踪关掉再重新处理，避免两种测试状态冲突。

**测试果杯**
这个是测试整机果杯逻辑/果杯状态的，不是重量参数下发。

重点：48 的重量设置页里，“测试果杯”发的是 FSM 指令：

```text
HC_CMD_TEST_CUP_ON
HC_CMD_TEST_CUP_OFF
```

而且目的地址是 `-1`，相当于发给 FSM/整机测试逻辑，不是单独发给 WAM。

所以我现在看到一个点：**鸿蒙这里如果把测试果杯发成 WAM 的 `0x0115/0x0116`，可能和 48 不一致。**  
内信号源发 WAM 是对的；测试果杯按 48 应该走 FSM 测试果杯指令。

---


**User**

这两个都是指令下发吗？

---


**OpenAI Codex**

是，**这两个都是指令下发**，但不是“参数结构体下发”。

区别是：

**内信号源**
是 WAM 控制指令下发：

```text
0x0113 内信号源开
0x0114 内信号源关
```

没有参数 payload，主要就是告诉 WAM：开启/关闭内部模拟触发。

**测试果杯**
也是控制指令下发。  
但按 48 的实现，它应该是 FSM 指令：

```text
HC_CMD_TEST_CUP_ON
HC_CMD_TEST_CUP_OFF
```

也是没有参数 payload，主要告诉 FSM 开启/关闭果杯测试逻辑。

所以一句话：**都是指令下发，不是数据参数下发。**  
内信号源发给 WAM；测试果杯按 48 应该发给 FSM。

---


**User**

OK  那这个G-AD系数 这个好像修改不了 然后就是当前重量 还有阈值 是根据啥来的

---


**OpenAI Codex**

我先看一下鸿蒙这个区域的控件绑定。你说的 G-AD、当前重量、阈值都在同一个页面里，关键是它们到底绑到哪个 `@State`，以及下发时写进哪个结构体。

---


**OpenAI Codex**

Codegraph 没抓到页面代码，我直接读 `WeightSettingsPage.ets`。

---


**OpenAI Codex**

现在清楚了：页面里有两个看起来像“G-AD系数”的东西，一个是上面的“校正系数”可编辑；G-AD框里“标定”右边那个值是显示计算结果的，当前写法确实不能直接输入。

---


**OpenAI Codex**

是的，你感觉对了：现在 **G-AD 系数那一栏不是直接编辑框**。

当前鸿蒙逻辑是：

**G-AD 系数来源**
从 WAM 返回的通道参数来：

```text
StWeightGlobal.Weights[channel].FGADParam[0]
```

页面里对应：

```text
correctionCoef = weight.fGADParam[0]
calibrationValue = weight.fGADParam[0]
```

下发时写回：

```text
StWeightBaseInfo.FGADParam[0] = correctionCoef
```

但是 UI 里有两处：

- 上面的 **“校正系数”** 是可编辑的，绑定 `correctionCoef`
- “G-AD系数(AD0)”里面“标定”右边那个框是 `calibrationValue`，现在是只读显示，不可直接输入

所以你说“G-AD系数修改不了”，应该是点到了下面那个只读框。要改的话现在只能改上面的“校正系数”，或者输入“重量 + AD值”点“标定”，它会算：

```text
校正系数 = 重量 / AD值
```

**当前重量、阈值来源**
优先从通道参数来：

```text
StWeightGlobal.Weights[channel].WaveInterval[0] -> 当前重量
StWeightGlobal.Weights[channel].WaveInterval[1] -> 阈值
```

同时全局参数里也有一份：

```text
StGlobalWeightBaseInfo.RefWeight -> 当前重量
StGlobalWeightBaseInfo.WeightTh  -> 阈值
```

但鸿蒙现在会先读全局的，然后马上被通道的 `WaveInterval` 覆盖掉。  
所以页面最终显示的“当前重量/阈值”，是当前通道 `WaveInterval[0]/[1]`。

**OpenAI Codex**

48 里关键点出来了：标定按钮只发通道 `HC_WAM_CMD_WEIGHT_INFO`，立即生效/保存会同时发通道参数和全局参数；而鸿蒙现在“发送后立刻回读”，会和真正发送到 WAM 并发，容易把旧值读回来。继续看具体保存代码。

**OpenAI Codex**

根因基本明确了：现在鸿蒙发完“标定/立即生效”后马上回读，而 Go 后端又把 WAM 指令放到 goroutine 里并发发。你日志里就是 `0x011D`、`0x011C`、`0x0110` 同时打过去，`0x011C` 直接失败。48 里不是这么干的，它通道参数发完后会等 1 秒再发全局参数。

**OpenAI Codex**

对，这个“不变”的主要原因我已经抓到了：不是单纯 UI 问题，是下发顺序和回读时机有问题。

你刚才日志里是这样：

```text
0x011D 通道参数发送
0x011C 全局参数发送
0x0110 立刻回读
```

而且几乎同一毫秒打过去，结果：

```text
0x011D success
0x011C result=-1
0x0110 success
```

这就会导致：通道参数可能刚发完，全局参数失败，然后马上回读旧数据，页面又被旧值覆盖。重启后当然还是旧的。

我改了两处：

- [websocket.go](E:/goTest/go/ohos/Tcp/websocket.go:829)：Go 后端 WAM 指令改成顺序执行，不再 goroutine 并发打 WAM。
- [WeightSettingsPage.ets](E:/new/my_harmony/entry/src/main/ets/components/dialogs/pages/WeightSettingsPage.ets:617)：鸿蒙“立即生效”现在先发通道参数，等 `1s` 再发全局参数；标定/立即生效后的回读也延迟 `1.5s`，避免读旧值。

48 里也是类似思路：发完 `HC_WAM_CMD_WEIGHT_INFO` 后，会 `sleep(1000)` 再发 `HC_WAM_CMD_GLOBAL_WEIGHT_INFO`。

你重新测的时候，日志应该变成这种顺序：

```text
saveWamWeightInfo ... 0x011D
saveWamWeightInfo success
约 1 秒后
saveWamGlobalWeightInfo ... 0x011C
saveWamGlobalWeightInfo success
再延迟后
wamGetInfo ... 0x0110
```

如果这三个都 success，但重启后还是旧值，那就不是发送顺序了，要继续看 WAM 是否真正把 `StWeightBaseInfo / StGlobalWeightBaseInfo` 持久化。

**User**

我有点不懂 这个标定和归零是什么东西 他不会下发吗？

---


**OpenAI Codex**

懂，你这个疑惑很正常。**标定**和**归零**不是一类东西。

**标定是什么**
标定是为了算出 G-AD 系数。

逻辑大概是：

```text
已知重量 / AD变化量 = G-AD系数
```

比如你放一个 100g 的标准物，当前 AD 值是 3000，零点 AD 是 1000：

```text
G-AD系数 = 100 / (3000 - 1000) = 0.05
```

然后这个系数会写进：

```text
StWeightBaseInfo.FGADParam[0]
```

所以**标定是会下发的**，下发的是：

```text
HC_WAM_CMD_WEIGHT_INFO 0x011D
payload = StWeightBaseInfo
```

也就是你日志里的：

```text
saveWamWeightInfo ... cmd=0x011D
```

**归零是什么**
归零不是改 G-AD 系数。归零是告诉 WAM：当前 AD 值作为零点/皮重基准。

它下发的是控制指令：

```text
HC_WAM_CMD_RESET_AD 0x011B
payload = StResetAD
```

所以**归零也会下发**，但它下发的不是 `StWeightBaseInfo`，而是“AD归零命令”。

**区别一句话**
```text
归零：确定零点 AD
标定：用标准重量和 AD 差值算 G-AD 系数，并下发系数
```

现在鸿蒙这里：
- 点“标定”会算 `correctionCoef`，然后发 `0x011D`
- 点“归零”会发 `0x011B`
- 点“立即生效”会发 `0x011D` 和 `0x011C`

如果你想看归零有没有下发，日志里应该找：

```text
wamResetAd
WAM cmd=0x011B
```

**OpenAI Codex**

所以不是 `0x011D` 没下发，也不是 WAM 完全没改。你重启后显示 `0.000000`，更像是鸿蒙启动时先收到了 FSM 的 `StGlobal`，里面的重量字段还是旧值/0，然后它把 WAM 的重量缓存覆盖掉了。

[GlobalDataInterface.ets](E:/new/my_harmony/entry/src/main/ets/protocol/GlobalDataInterface.ets:1181)

现在逻辑变成：

- `StGlobal` 里的重量字段只作为兜底
- 一旦收到 WAM 回读，或者本地刚编辑过重量参数，就不再允许 FSM 的旧 `StGlobal` 覆盖它
- 清空数据时会一起清掉这个标记

你重新跑后，重启进入页面时可能短暂显示旧值，但等 `WAM__CMD_WEIGHT_INFO(0x0120)` 回包后，应该更新成：

我查下来，确实还有两个前端问题，不是你操作的问题。


```text

```

我已经补了 `standardADValue`，点“归零”后会记录当前 AD，点“标定”时用 AD 差值计算。

```text

点立即生效
```

你之前日志里 WAM 回读已经有新值：

```text
FGADParam=[0.030700 0.500000]
```

Key recent state/edits already made:
1. Go backend WAM logging and sequencing:
   - `go/ohos/Tcp/websocket.go`
   - Added “WebSocket 收到 saveWamWeightInfo/saveWamGlobalWeightInfo” logs with payload fields.
   - Changed WAM handlers from goroutines to synchronous execution:
     - `handleSimpleWAMCommand`, `handleSimpleWAMChannelCommand`, `handleWAMResetAD`, `handleWAMWeightInfoData`, `handleWAMGlobalWeightInfoData`
   - `handleWAMGlobalWeightInfoData` logs and sleeps `1000ms` before sending global weight, matching 48’s delay after channel weight write.
   - `sendWAMCommand` already logs sending/success/failure.
2. Go WAM readback logging:
   - `go/ohos/Tcp/ctcpserver.go`
   - In `cmdWAMWeightGlobal` (`0x0120`) case, added `CTCP StWeightGlobal 回读` log printing `GWeight` fields and `weight0` `FGADParam/FTemperatureParams/WaveInterval`.
3. Harmony weight page changed:
   - `E:/new/my_harmony/entry/src/main/ets/components/dialogs/pages/WeightSettingsPage.ets`
   - Added `wamReadbackDelayMs = 1500`, `sleep()`, and delayed readback after 标定 and 立即生效.
   - `handleApplyNow` sends channel then global immediately; Go backend now provides ordered/settled execution.
   - Added `standardADValue` state.
   - `handleZero()` now records current `adValueInput` as `standardADValue` and sets `calibrationValue='0.000000'`.
   - `updateCalibrationValueFromInputs()` now uses `weightInput / (AD - standardADValue)`, aligning with 48’s `weight / (GAD0ADtextBox - m_nStandardAD0)`.
   - G-AD display beside 标定 changed from `buildPlainInput()` to editable `buildEditableInput()`, writing directly to `correctionCoef` and `calibrationValue`.
4. Harmony `GlobalDataInterface.ets` changed:
   - Added `latestWeightGlobalDirectByDevice: Map<number, boolean>`.
   - Public `updateWeightGlobal()` marks data as direct (`true`).
   - `syncWeightGlobalFromGlobalConfig()` now only uses FSM `StGlobal` fallback if no direct WAM/local weight data exists, to avoid stale `StGlobal` overriding WAM `0x0120` readbacks.
   - `clearData()` clears this flag.
5. Earlier relevant work (before latest checkpoint):
   - Added `StGlobal.gweight` and `StGlobal.weights`, and mapped `GWeight/Weights` in `StGlobalJsonMapper.ets`, so FSM `StGlobal` can seed weight settings before WAM readback.
   - Go backend has WAM command support:
     - `0x0110` `cTCPHCWAMWeightOn` for `wamGetInfo`
     - `0x011B` reset AD
     - `0x011C` global weight info
     - `0x011D` channel weight info
   - `WeightSettingsPage` buttons already wire reset/internal signal/test cup/wave/data tracking/apply.
   - Card drag/drop bug fixed earlier: `LiquidCardsArea.ets` deep clones after manager updates; `ThirdLayer.ets` renders from `chartDataStrings` even if `chartData` empty.

Important logs/evidence user provided:
- WAM readback after calibration showed WAM did have new values:
  ```text
  CTCP StWeightGlobal 回读 ... gWeight{... RefWeight=124, WeightTh=228}, weight0{FGADParam=[0.030700 0.500000], FTemperatureParams=12.000000, WaveInterval=[124 228]}
  ```
  So WAM write/readback worked at least once. The restart display issue was likely UI/cache overwrite or UI binding issue, not total WAM failure.
- Before sequencing fix, logs had `0x011D`, `0x011C`, `0x0110` nearly simultaneous, with `0x011C result=-1`.
- After sequencing, `0x011D` and `0x011C` succeeded, but an extra early `wamGetInfo` could still appear if frontend gaps allowed it; moved the 1s wait to Go backend to preserve ordering.

48 reference findings already gathered:
- `projectsetform.cpp`:
  - `on_SingnalSourcecheckBox_stateChanged`: 内信号源 sends WAM `HC_WAM_CMD_SIMULATEDPULSE_ON/OFF` to `CommonFunction::GetWAMID(nowSelSysIdx)` and disables data tracking.
  - `on_TestFruitCupcheckBox_clicked`: 测试果杯 sends FSM command `HC_CMD_TEST_CUP_ON/OFF` with dest `-1`, only if `GlobalDataInterface::global_IsTestMode`.
  - `WeightSetPageUnSelected`: turns off 内信号源 and 测试果杯 when leaving page.
  - `on_GAD0Zerobutton_clicked`: sends WAM `HC_WAM_CMD_RESET_AD`, records `m_nStandardAD0 = GAD0ADtextBox`, sets display to `0.000000`.
  - `on_GAD0Calibratbutton_clicked`: computes `fGADParam[0] = GAD0Weight / (GAD0AD - m_nStandardAD0)`, updates `globalOut_WeightBaseInfo`, sends WAM `HC_WAM_CMD_WEIGHT_INFO`.
  - `InitWeightSetForm` around 9511/9586 uses `tempGlobalWeightBaseInfo[m_WeightSubsysindex].RefWeight` and `WeightTh` for “当前重量/阈值”.
  - Weight readback uses `weight.waveinterval[0/1]` for wave capture `m_WaveInterval`, not necessarily for displayed 当前重量/阈值.
  - `GlobalWeightInfoSaveConfig(false)` sends selected channel `HC_WAM_CMD_WEIGHT_INFO`, sleeps `1000ms`, then sends `HC_WAM_CMD_GLOBAL_WEIGHT_INFO` for each subsystem.
- `interface.h`:
  - `StWeightBaseInfo` fields: `fGADParam[2]` (G-AD系数 AD0/AD1), `fTemperatureParams`, `waveinterval[2]`
  - `StGlobalWeightBaseInfo` fields include `RefWeight`, `WeightTh`
  - WAM commands: `HC_WAM_CMD_RESET_AD`, `HC_WAM_CMD_GLOBAL_WEIGHT_INFO`, `HC_WAM_CMD_WEIGHT_INFO`
  - FSM commands include `HC_CMD_TEST_CUP_ON/OFF`

Current code-review findings to report (evidence collected):
1. **High: 测试果杯 target is wrong vs 48.**
   - Harmony `WeightSettingsPage.ets:478-481` calls `sendWamTestCupOn/Off(this.getSelectedWamId())`.
   - `ConfigSender.ets:384-398` sends WAM test cup.
   - 48 `projectsetform.cpp:9681` sends FSM `HC_CMD_TEST_CUP_ON/OFF` to dest `-1`, not WAM. It also gates on test mode and turns it off on page leave.
   - Risk: Harmony may command wrong board; UI “测试果杯” behavior won’t match machine behavior.
2. **High/Medium: 当前重量/阈值 source likely wrong.**
   - Harmony `syncStateFromWeightSnapshot()` first sets from `gweight.RefWeight/WeightTh`, then overwrites:
     - `WeightSettingsPage.ets:339-340` `currentWeight = weight.waveinterval[0]`, `threshold = weight.waveinterval[1]`.
   - 48 displays current weight/threshold from `tempGlobalWeightBaseInfo.RefWeight/WeightTh` (`projectsetform.cpp:9511-9513`, `9586-9587`). `waveinterval` is used as `m_WaveInterval` for wave capture/save, not necessarily the visible current weight/threshold.
   - Risk: UI may show/save channel wave interval as current weight/threshold incorrectly, especially if those values diverge.
3. **Medium: Ack handling still not real.**
   - `ConfigSender.ets:634-668` WAM tracked methods return `sendOk` from WebSocket send only, `ackTracked: true`, `ackHandle: null`. `WeightSettingsPage` uses `sendOk` to mark success and update local cache.
   - Go does send `commandAck`, but frontend does not await/bind it.
   - Risk: UI can show success and cache values even if Go later logs `result=-1`; this has happened in user logs.
4. **Medium: `zeroValue` is semantically wrong/confusing.**
   - Harmony uses `zeroValue` as `weight.fGADParam[1]` (`WeightSettingsPage.ets:337`, `429`, `926-929`), displayed under a “归零” row.
   - 48’s `fGADParam[0]` and `[1]` are AD0/AD1 coefficients, not zero offset. Actual zero baseline is runtime `m_nStandardAD0/m_nStandardAD1`.
   - Risk: editing/“清零” may unintentionally modify AD1 coefficient, not zero offset; labels are misleading. If only AD0 is supported, this row is wrong.
5. **Medium/Low: Multiple subsystem global weight handling simplified.**
   - Harmony `buildGlobalWeightPayload()` writes the same `totalCupCount` to all `nTotalCupNums` slots and sends one WAM global to selected WAM.
   - 48 updates selected/mirrored indices and sends global weight info to every subsystem (or every pair under MAX64).
   - If only one subsystem currently, okay; otherwise incomplete.
6. **Medium: Test/temporary state cleanup missing.**
   - 48 `WeightSetPageUnSelected()` turns off 内信号源, 测试果杯, and data tracking on page leave.
   - Harmony `aboutToDisappear()` only removes listeners. It does not turn off toggles.
   - Risk: WAM/FSM test states can remain active after leaving page.
7. **Potential UI bug: G-AD “标定” right-side input now editable; ensure no duplicate `校正系数` field confusion.**
   - There are now two fields for same `correctionCoef`: top “校正系数” and G-AD display box. This may be okay but UI can confuse users.

**OpenAI Codex**

目前已经看到几个明显不对齐的点：测试果杯、当前重量/阈值、以及“发送成功”和“设备执行成功”的判断不是一回事。我再把关键代码段定位一下，避免靠印象下结论。

---


**OpenAI Codex**

这里不像单纯的“页面没刷出来”，更像几个字段含义被混在一起了：有些是 WAM 通道参数，有些是 WAM 全局参数，还有一个测试果杯其实走 FSM。继续对照 48 的具体函数。

---


**OpenAI Codex**

另外一个关键点：48 里 “G-AD系数(AD0)” 这一块的控件命名很迷惑，但代码能看出含义。右侧“标定”框更像实时称重显示，不是保存字段；真正保存的是 `fGADParam[0]`。鸿蒙这里把它当成可编辑保存值了，这会解释你说的重启后显示不对。

---


**OpenAI Codex**

还有一个小但危险的类型点：你这个版本如果按 48 的 `BL4` 分支，`WeightTh` 是 `ushort`，鸿蒙现在下发时却按 0-255 截断。数值不大时看不出来，超过 255 就会“改了又像没改”。

---


**OpenAI Codex**

我又确认了一下 Go 结构体：这里确实还按 `uint8` 解析/编码 `WeightTh`，和 48 `BL4` 的 `ushort` 分支不一致。这个不是 UI 样式问题，是 wire 结构体版本问题。

---


**OpenAI Codex**

**结论**

我看完了，这个重量设置界面还不算正确。现在是“部分能下发”，但字段语义和 48 没完全对齐，所以你感觉有问题是对的。

**主要问题**

1. **高：测试果杯发错对象了**
   鸿蒙现在是 WAM 指令：  
   [WeightSettingsPage.ets](E:/new/my_harmony/entry/src/main/ets/components/dialogs/pages/WeightSettingsPage.ets:478) 调 `sendWamTestCupOn/Off`，后端走 `wamTestCupOn`。
   
   但 48 是 FSM 指令：  
   [projectsetform.cpp](E:/new/48/RSS/Forms/projectsetform.cpp:9681) 发 `HC_CMD_TEST_CUP_ON/OFF`，目标是 `-1`。  
   所以“测试果杯”现在不应该发 WAM。

2. **高：当前重量/阈值被 `waveinterval` 覆盖了**
   鸿蒙先读 `gweight.RefWeight / WeightTh`，然后又被通道的 `weight.waveinterval[0/1]` 覆盖：  
   [WeightSettingsPage.ets](E:/new/my_harmony/entry/src/main/ets/components/dialogs/pages/WeightSettingsPage.ets:330)
   
   48 里当前重量/阈值来自全局重量参数：  
   [projectsetform.cpp](E:/new/48/RSS/Forms/projectsetform.cpp:9511)  
   `waveinterval` 是波形参数，不是当前重量/阈值。这个会导致显示和保存都串字段。

3. **高：G-AD/标定/归零这一块字段映射不对**
   48 结构体里 `fGADParam[0] / [1]` 是 AD0/AD1 的 G-AD 系数：  
   [interface.h](E:/new/48/RSS/Base/interface.h:8419)
   
   但鸿蒙现在把 `fGADParam[1]` 当成“归零值”：  
   [WeightSettingsPage.ets](E:/new/my_harmony/entry/src/main/ets/components/dialogs/pages/WeightSettingsPage.ets:337)  
   [WeightSettingsPage.ets](E:/new/my_harmony/entry/src/main/ets/components/dialogs/pages/WeightSettingsPage.ets:429)
   
   这会导致 AD0 页面实际在改 AD1 系数。你说“标定和归零重启后不对”，这里就是核心原因之一。

4. **中：前端没有真正等设备 ack**
   Go 后端会回 `commandAck`：  
   [websocket.go](E:/goTest/go/ohos/Tcp/websocket.go:896)
   
   但鸿蒙只是打印 ack，没有把结果返回给页面：  
   [HarmonyWebSocketClient.ets](E:/new/my_harmony/entry/src/main/ets/utils/network/HarmonyWebSocketClient.ets:1035)
   
   页面用的是 `sendOk`，也就是“WebSocket 消息发给 Go 成功”，不是“WAM 执行成功”。所以后端如果 `result=-1`，页面也可能显示成功并更新本地缓存。

5. **中：离开页面没有关闭测试状态**
   48 离开重量页会关闭内信号源、测试果杯、数据追踪：  
   [projectsetform.cpp](E:/new/48/RSS/Forms/projectsetform.cpp:10231)
   
   鸿蒙现在 `aboutToDisappear()` 只移除监听：  
   [WeightSettingsPage.ets](E:/new/my_harmony/entry/src/main/ets/components/dialogs/pages/WeightSettingsPage.ets:109)

6. **中：`WeightTh` 类型可能还没按你的版本对齐**
   Go 里现在是 `uint8`：  
   [ctcp_structs.go](E:/goTest/go/ohos/Tcp/ctcp_structs.go:219)
   
   48 的 `BL4` 分支是 `ushort`：  
   [interface.h](E:/new/48/RSS/Base/interface.h:8497)
   
   这个要按你实际 L4/BL4 宏确认；如果你的设备实际走 `ushort`，现在阈值高字节会丢。

**已经对的部分**

`立即生效` 确实有下发链路：通道参数走 `0x011D`，全局重量参数走 `0x011C`。`归零` 也确实有 `0x011B RESET_AD`。问题不是“完全没发”，而是页面字段含义、测试果杯命令域、ack 判断这几块没对齐。

我没跑编译，按你项目说明没有帮你编译。

**OpenAI Codex**

**User**

什么情况

---


**OpenAI Codex**

没出问题，第一项代码已经改进去了。我正在核对一个细节：48 的目标是 `-1`，Go 里用 `destId` 推目标 IP，如果 `-1` 直接参与 IP 计算可能会跑偏；我马上把这个目标路由也处理稳。

---


**OpenAI Codex**

我找到具体原因了：`destId=-1` 如果直接拿来算 IP，会变成 `192.168.0.240` 这种错目标。所以修法是：包里的 `destId` 仍然按 48 发 `-1`，但 TCP 连接目标用当前选中的 FSM。这样既保留 48 的命令语义，也能连到正确机器。

---


**OpenAI Codex**

这下语义对了：前端发送当前 FSM 作为连接目标提示，同时 packet 的 `destId` 仍然是 `-1`。我再静态核对一下调用链。
